[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 猞assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m To find the expected win, we need to consider the probabilities of each outcome and the corresponding winnings.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m First, let's find the probability of selecting a black ball from bin $A$. There is only one white ball and four black balls, so the probability is $\frac{1}{5}$.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m Next, let's find the probability of selecting a white ball from bin $A$. There is one white ball and four black balls, so the probability is $\frac{1}{5}$.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m

[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m Finally, let's find the probability of selecting a ball from bin $W$ given that a white ball was selected from bin $A$. There are five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$, so the probability is $\frac{6}{5}$.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m Now we can calculate the expected win by multiplying the probability of each outcome by the corresponding winnings and summing them up:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m

You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 3. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) given that a black ball is selected from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 4. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) given that a white ball is selected from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Bin \( W \) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 5. **Expected win calculation:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The expected win \( E \) is the sum of the products of the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings. We can express this as:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = P(\text{Black from } A) \times P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) \times \text{Winnings from } B + P(\text{White from } A) \times P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) \times \text{Winnings from } W
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Substituting the values we have:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \left( \frac{4}{5} \right) \times \left( \frac{3}{4} \right) \times 1 + \left( \frac{1}{5} \right) \times \left( \frac{1}{6} \right) \times 7
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 6. **Simplify the expression:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{4}{5} \times \frac{3}{4} \times 1 + \frac{1}{5} \times \frac{1}{6} \times 7
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{7}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 7. **Find a common denominator and add the fractions:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The common denominator for 5 and 30 is 30.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{3 \times 6}{30} + \frac{7}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{18}{30} + \frac{7}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{25}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m

You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities and the corresponding winnings for each possible outcome. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 3. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) given a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \( A \), a ball is randomly selected from bin \( B \). Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 4. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) given a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \( A \), a ball is randomly selected from bin \( W \). Bin \( W \) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 5. **Expected win calculation:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The expected win \( E \) is the sum of the products of the probabilities and the corresponding winnings. We can express this as:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = P(\text{Black from } A) \cdot P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) \cdot \text{Winnings from Ball from } B + P(\text{White from } A) \cdot P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) \cdot \text{Winnings from Ball from } W
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Substituting the values we have:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \left( \frac{4}{5} \right) \left( \frac{3}{4} \right) \cdot 1 + \left( \frac{1}{5} \right) \left( \frac{5}{6} \right) \cdot 7
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Simplifying each term:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{4 \cdot 3}{5 \cdot 4} + \frac{1 \cdot 5}{5 \cdot 6} \cdot 7 = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{5}{30} \cdot 7 = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{35}{30} = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{7}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    To add these fractions, we need a common denominator. The least common multiple of 5 and 6 is 30:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E = \frac{3 \cdot 6}{5 \cdot 6} + \frac{7 \cdot 5}{6 \cdot 5} = \frac{18}{30} + \frac{35}{30} = \frac{53}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m Therefore, the expected win is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m \boxed{\frac{53}{30}}

[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities and the corresponding winnings for each possible outcome. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Bin \(A\) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \(A\), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \(B\). Bin \(B\) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$1 from bin \(B\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\$1 | \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$7 from bin \(B\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\$7 | \text{Black from } A) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a black ball is selected from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E(\$1 | \text{Black from } A) \cdot P(\$1 | \text{Black from } A) + E(\$7 | \text{Black from } A) \cdot P(\$7 | \text{Black from } A) = 1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + 7 \cdot \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = 3
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \(A\), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \(W\). Bin \(W\) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$8 from bin \(W\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\$8 | \text{White from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$500 from bin \(W\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\$500 | \text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a white ball is selected from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E(\$8 | \text{White from } A) \cdot P(\$8 | \text{White from } A) + E(\$500 | \text{White from } A) \cdot P(\$500 | \text{White from } A) = 8 \cdot \frac{5}{6} + 500 \cdot \frac{1}{6} = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = 90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 3. **Total expected win:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The total expected win is the weighted average of the expected wins from both scenarios, weighted by their respective probabilities:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E(\text{Total Win}) = P(\text{Black from } A) \cdot E(\$1 | \text{Black from } A) + P(\text{White from } A) \cdot E(\$8 | \text{White from } A) = \frac{4}{5} \cdot 3 + \frac{1}{5} \cdot 90 = \frac{12}{5} + \frac{90}{5} = \frac{102}{5} = 20.4
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m Therefore, the expected win is \(\boxed{20.4}\).

[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities and the corresponding winnings for each possible outcome. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \( A \), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \( B \). Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$1 from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\$1 | \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$7 from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    P(\$7 | \text{Black from } A) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a black ball is selected from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    E(\$1 | \text{Black from } A) \cdot P(\$1 | \text{Black from } A) + E(\$7 | \text{Black from } A) \cdot P(\$7 | \text{Black from } A) = \$1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + \$7 \cdot \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \$5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=1110387)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
